	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh') != 'd322a3efbaf4dbfe0615edb182fa2bbb1b98f2a3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh') !== 'd322a3efbaf4dbfe0615edb182fa2bbb1b98f2a3') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh') !== '0423a7eff554a021f252b3ccd07497a89bfc8bd9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh') !== 'd322a3efbaf4dbfe0615edb182fa2bbb1b98f2a3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/901_vnag_version_check/vnag.sh');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '6a57dedbc5a81748c0173c079f9da10705824e1c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '6a57dedbc5a81748c0173c079f9da10705824e1c') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'a723e1167338869b18c44a7eb90f11e6d15629c4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '6a57dedbc5a81748c0173c079f9da10705824e1c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
